  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_f165c1ff-a0b3-4dc2-86b9-6e8b3935b72b'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

<span id="freeTextContainer2064008972693022404">A thousand years ago, two young lovers were betrayed-Alger Waterlow to his death, and Hanalea, Queen of the Fells, to a life without love. <br/><br/>Now, once again, the Queendom of the Fells seems likely to shatter apart. For young queen Raisa <i>ana'</i>Marianna, maintaining peace even within her own castle walls is nearly impossible; tension between wizards and Clan has reached a fevere</span>
  <span id="freeText2064008972693022404" style="display:none">A thousand years ago, two young lovers were betrayed-Alger Waterlow to his death, and Hanalea, Queen of the Fells, to a life without love. <br /><br />Now, once again, the Queendom of the Fells seems likely to shatter apart. For young queen Raisa <i>ana'</i>Marianna, maintaining peace even within her own castle walls is nearly impossible; tension between wizards and Clan has reached a fevered pitch. With surrounding kingdoms seeking to prey on the Fells' inner turmoil, Raisa's best hope is to unite her people against a common enemy. But that enemy might be the person with whom she's falling in love.<br /><br />Through a complicated web of lies and unholy alliances, former streetlord Han Alister has become a member of the Wizard Council of the Fells. Navigating the cut-throat world of blue blood politics has never been more dangerous, and Han seems to inspire hostility among Clan and wizards alike. His only ally is the queen, and despite the perils involved, Han finds it impossible to ignore his feelings for Raisa. Before long, Han finds himself in possession of a secret believed to be lost to history, a discovery powerful enough to unite the people of the Fells. But will the secret die with him before he can use it? <br /><br />A simple, devastating truth concealed by a thousand-year-old lie at last comes to light in this stunning conclusion to the Seven Realms series.</span>

<div id="review_1170312042" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1170312042" />
    <a title="Katerina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina"><img alt="Katerina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1470667070p2/5014021.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1170312042?book_show_action=true">Jan 16, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katerina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katerina" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina">Katerina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1170312042" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5864470585443981573">That feeling when you finish an <b>incredible</b> series<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469002216ra/19767768.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>but then you realize you have to say goodbye <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469002216ra/19767769.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Mix the previous images and you have me. In the middle of the night. Trying to stay awake. Stomach grumbling with hunger.<br/>It's the best feeling ever!<br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“History is written by the victors. The truth is, the villains were less villainous, and the heroes less heroic, than you’ve been told.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>A thousand years ago, Alger Waterlow fell in love with Hanalea, the Queen of the Fells. But their love was do</span>
  <span id="freeText5864470585443981573" style="display:none">That feeling when you finish an <b>incredible</b> series<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469002216ra/19767768.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>but then you realize you have to say goodbye <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469002216ra/19767769.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Mix the previous images and you have me. In the middle of the night. Trying to stay awake. Stomach grumbling with hunger.<br>It's the best feeling ever!<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“History is written by the victors. The truth is, the villains were less villainous, and the heroes less heroic, than you’ve been told.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>A thousand years ago, Alger Waterlow fell in love with Hanalea, the Queen of the Fells. But their love was doomed from the start. Betrayed, tortured and imprisoned in an amulet, Alger was demonized by history. He became the Demon King, and Hanalea the brave warrior that rid the world of this evil. But history has its way of repeating itself. Raisa <i>ana'</i>Marianna is now the Queen of the Fells, and her reign is more fragile than ever. She has to prevent the clans from turning against the wizards while an enemy from the south is ready to march and everyone questions the 17 years old queen's capability of rising up to the challenge. And she eventually has to marry someone for political reasons and ignore her heart that beats for Han Alister, the only person the clans and the wizards hate with a loathing passion and may be responsible for heinous crimes. Han Alister on the other hand is determined to marry Raisa, even if that means allying with untrustworthy people and trying to find a mythical armory with weapons of terrific potential, while everyone accuses him of murder. <i>Will Han and Raisa manage to save the queendom without sacrificing their love in the process?</i><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I am a Gray Wolf queen. We have never been graceful losers. And so, I do not intend to lose. I will fight you until the last breath leaves my body. You will not take me alive.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>I love fantasy.</b> It's always been my favorite genre, and books like <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8069828.The_Crimson_Crown__Seven_Realms___4_" title="The Crimson Crown (Seven Realms, #4) by Cinda Williams Chima" rel="nofollow noopener">The Crimson Crown</a> are the reason why. You can close your eyes and picture <b>seiges</b> and <b>secret tunnels</b> under the mountains and <b>battles</b> and <b>illicit kisses</b> under the brilliance of the moon. You can weild a sword like a warrior even though you've never seen one up close, you can feel the magic burning in your fingers waiting to be unleashed even though you're a mundane, you attend meetings that determine the fate of a nation you've never heard of, and you can do all these things because one person's pen is more powerful than a wand. People like <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/125308.Cinda_Williams_Chima" title="Cinda Williams Chima" rel="nofollow noopener">Cinda Williams Chima</a> are my heroes.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441685146ra/16138588.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8069828.The_Crimson_Crown__Seven_Realms___4_" title="The Crimson Crown (Seven Realms, #4) by Cinda Williams Chima" rel="nofollow noopener">The Crimson Crown</a> the stakes are higher than ever, and I am so proud that both Han and Raisa rose up to the circumstances. <b>Politics, war and magic</b>, <b>adventure and romance</b>, The Crimson Crown is a blend of everything you could wish for in a YA fantasy book! The characters are not good or evil, they're always somewhere in between. Everyone wants to protect the people he or she is responsible for, from the Demonai warriors to wizards and council members and simple soldiers. Of course you'll hate some of them for their decisions, for messing with your heroes, but you can understand why they act this way, and for me that is a huge achievement. Take Micah, for instance. I still can't make up my mind about him because he tried to sink my ship many times, but I can't label him as a villain and that's kind of frustrating. Hating him would be easier.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Complicated. And yet—simple. They were like two pieces of a failed star, drawn together by a shared history and a memory of illicit kisses.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>At first I was cautious of shipping Han and Raisa because they've proven that they will kiss anyone with a set of lips (is there a thing such as kissing addiction? Raisa could be suffering from it, just saying) but I was pleasantly surprised by the way their relationship developed. Raisa stood up for Han even when the entire world was against him, she put her faith in him and supported him, while Han did everything in his power, fought enemies and allies to secure a future with her. So yes, I ended up shipping them. Hard. With butterflies and giggling and all that stuff.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“But I don't want your throne."<br>"Then what do you want?"<br>"You.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I didn't cry during the entire series, but I did cry in the last two pages. It was the most suitable way to finish a story that started when two lovers were torn apart a thousand of years ago. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/125308.Cinda_Williams_Chima" title="Cinda Williams Chima" rel="nofollow noopener">Cinda Williams Chima</a>, you are a true sorceress!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1430832551ra/14767080.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="5864470585443981573" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1010899628" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1010899628" />
    <a title="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31461418-alienor-french-frowner"><img alt="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1532688964p2/31461418.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1010899628?book_show_action=true">Jul 29, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" href="/user/show/31461418-alienor-french-frowner">Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=knots-in-my-stomach">knots-in-my-stomach</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=epic-reads-for-light-and-dark-pup">epic-reads-for-light-and-dark-pup</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=2016-reads">2016-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=fave-characters">fave-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=alternative-pov">alternative-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=fave-ya-and-fantasy">fave-ya-and-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=romance-i-root-for">romance-i-root-for</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1010899628" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5583958736494669379"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457478211i/18364773._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>✨ <b>Spoiler free for the whole series</b> ✨<br/><br/><b>LOOK OUT, FANTASY WRITERS!</b> SEE THIS BOOK? <br/><br/>*pushes <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8069828.The_Crimson_Crown__Seven_Realms___4_' title='The Crimson Crown (Seven Realms, #4) by Cinda Williams Chima' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Crimson Crown</a> in your hands*<br/><br/><b>SEE THIS?</b> <br/><br/>LOOK AT IT! JUST LOOK AT IT! <br/><br/><b>This is <i>how</i> you end a series : BLOODY. <i>FABULOUS</i>.</b> <br/><br/>WHY? WHAT DO WE READERS WANT? <br/><br/>Alright. I can think of some things : <br/><br/><b>1)</b> <b>WE ARE OUT FOR BLOOD</b>. SO. We need <i>IN YOUR FACE!</i> moments with the villains and all those who annoyed the hell out of us. Yes, this is MUCH needed. Nothing's worst than anticlimactic confrontations. Give us GIDDINESS. <br/><br/><b>2)</b> <b>If </b></span>
  <span id="freeText5583958736494669379" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457478211i/18364773._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>✨ <b>Spoiler free for the whole series</b> ✨<br><br><b>LOOK OUT, FANTASY WRITERS!</b> SEE THIS BOOK? <br><br>*pushes <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8069828.The_Crimson_Crown__Seven_Realms___4_" title="The Crimson Crown (Seven Realms, #4) by Cinda Williams Chima" rel="nofollow noopener">The Crimson Crown</a> in your hands*<br><br><b>SEE THIS?</b> <br><br>LOOK AT IT! JUST LOOK AT IT! <br><br><b>This is <i>how</i> you end a series : BLOODY. <i>FABULOUS</i>.</b> <br><br>WHY? WHAT DO WE READERS WANT? <br><br>Alright. I can think of some things : <br><br><b>1)</b> <b>WE ARE OUT FOR BLOOD</b>. SO. We need <i>IN YOUR FACE!</i> moments with the villains and all those who annoyed the hell out of us. Yes, this is MUCH needed. Nothing's worst than anticlimactic confrontations. Give us GIDDINESS. <br><br><b>2)</b> <b>If you want to give us a romance, PLEASE SLOW DOWN</b>, because the butterflies, here? They would never have had the same impact if not for the wait. My ship made me suffer along the way, but it paid up x1000. <br><br><b>3)</b> <b>NO NEED FOR CARDBOARD PEOPLE</b>. Give us fleshed-out and interesting secondary characters - some we love to hate and other we'd defend with our *fictional* life. <br><br><b>4)</b> <b>We also need EPIC ENDINGS</b>. No <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7260188.Mockingjay__The_Hunger_Games___3_" title="Mockingjay (The Hunger Games, #3) by Suzanne Collins" rel="nofollow noopener">Mockingjay</a> "I don't know if my ship really sailed or what". No dull as hell temporizing like <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16150831.In_The_Afterlight__The_Darkest_Minds___3_" title="In The Afterlight (The Darkest Minds, #3) by Alexandra Bracken" rel="nofollow noopener">In The Afterlight</a> (I know, I gave it 5 stars at the time... I wouldn't now, honestly). The last book should always be the BEST of the series. If you want 600 pages of great battles, though, look elsewhere. This is not what it is about and I'm so glad it isn't. Alright, it is fairly predictable, but again, <b>I. Don't. Care.</b> Any book that manages to engross me like this deserves its 5 stars. Now, maybe I'm bewitched, and many readers will argue that nothing really happens and ... you know what? <b>Perhaps that's just the point. It is <i>not</i> so easy to bewitch me, if I dare say.</b><br><br><b>5)</b> Last but not least, you wouldn't want us to be disappointed in our main characters now would you? Take 3 stereotypes and call it a hero? Use idiotic misunderstandings to drive them through a painful joke of character development? NOPE. You do NOT want this. <b>Try this instead : give us flawed characters in whom we can believe. Now make them grow. Then again. Then <i>again</i></b>. Now perhaps, if you're lucky, you'll have Raisa and Han - I just freaking LOVE them. Here are characters who know what that means to have a backbone. <br><br>Of course <b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8069828.The_Crimson_Crown__Seven_Realms___4_" title="The Crimson Crown (Seven Realms, #4) by Cinda Williams Chima" rel="nofollow noopener">The Crimson Crown</a> passed all these tests with flying colors</b>. <br><br>Damn, I'm exhausted, I just <i>know</i> that a huge book hangover is coming, but it was <i>so</i> worth it. <br><br><i>For more of my reviews, please visit:</i><br><blockquote>
  <a href="https://meetthebookworld.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487851828i/22057164._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="5583958736494669379" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1713441106" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1713441106" />
    <a title="C.G. Drews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11375137-c-g-drews"><img alt="C.G. Drews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1521552918p2/11375137.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1713441106?book_show_action=true">Jul 30, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="C.G. Drews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="C.G. Drews" href="/user/show/11375137-c-g-drews">C.G. Drews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=5-star">5-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=epic-fantasy">epic-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=read-2016">read-2016</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1713441106" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6117037673463103603">My complete and very sensible reaction to this book is: <b>AFDSKJAFLDAJ I AM SO OBSESSED I MIGHT EXPLODE.</b> Like, omg, honestly this series has <i>stolen my heart</i>. I'm SO happy with the finale! I mean, it wasn't perfect and it was faaaar too long and got draggy there in the middle: BUT IT WAS <i>STILL EXCELLENT</i>. It was feelsy. I actually made psychotic fangirl noises. TWICE. My ship. Ohhhhhh my ship. And there was stabbing and torture as well so #winning<br/><br/>Who is that puddle on the floor howling about their f</span>
  <span id="freeText6117037673463103603" style="display:none">My complete and very sensible reaction to this book is: <b>AFDSKJAFLDAJ I AM SO OBSESSED I MIGHT EXPLODE.</b> Like, omg, honestly this series has <i>stolen my heart</i>. I'm SO happy with the finale! I mean, it wasn't perfect and it was faaaar too long and got draggy there in the middle: BUT IT WAS <i>STILL EXCELLENT</i>. It was feelsy. I actually made psychotic fangirl noises. TWICE. My ship. Ohhhhhh my ship. And there was stabbing and torture as well so #winning<br /><br />Who is that puddle on the floor howling about their feelings?<br /><br />OH THAT IS ME. IT'S OKAY. I'M PROBABLY DEAD.<br /><br /><b>What I really REALLY love about this series is how it balances everything!</b> Like we have the epic battles, the conspiracy theories, the magical-mentor-to-student lessons, the politics (SO MUCH OF THOSE) and the betrayals....and the romance. Like when am I one to swoon over romance? Pfft. Never. Except for this series apparently.<br /><br /><b>I swear Raisa and Han Alister are my ultimate OTP.</b> (At least for, like, this moment.) THEY ARE SO DOOMED TO NEVER BE TOGETHER. And they fight. And they betray each other. And they love each other <i>so fiercely</i> I am just literally exploding. CUE DERANGED FANGIRL NOISES. And honestly <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I'm usually not one to say "yes the 18 year olds should get married" but HELL YES I CHEERED WHEN THEY GOT MARRIED AT THE END. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><b> Perfect ship is perfect.</b> And by "perfect" I mean they totally hurt me but I'll forgive them.<br /><br /><b>There is a TON of plot going down here too.</b> Like that weird/creepy neighbouring king starts making trouble, and there's rebellions and fires, and the Demonai camp is being a TOTAL THISTLE IN THE BUTT. I love how it stuffed so much happenings in.<br /><br /><b>And IT HURT.</b> Did I mention torture and bleeding?!? (Although, tbh, I'm going to sound like a complete psychopath....but I think the torture was totally brushed over. ahem.) And Raisa is like still being pressure by everyone to marry. <br /><br />And Han is like "RUN AWAY WITH ME."<br />Raisa: "We'd never make it 5 miles"<br /><br />^^^ Okay that totally <i>did not happen</i> but the gist is there. #HungerGamesMoment<br /><br /><b>I also love how the magic is done.</b> It's actually complex (the whole world is complex!!!!!) and I just get so invested in how they do magic and the amulets and the charms and jinxes and afsjdkalj. It is one of my favourite magic systems of EVER.<br /><br /><b>OTHER RANDOM STUFF I LOVED:</b><br />• Han went <i>soooo</i> dark side occasionally and I freaking love it.<br />• He is a handsome devil. (Pretty as the devil and twice as clever? &lt;-- Han)<br />• HAN HAN HAN HAN HAN<br />• I also love the street slang. It's so easy to grasp and so flawlessly slipped in. <br />• There was a bit of a murder mystery happening too. LOVE IT.<br />• Any scene with Dancer is epic. I'm glad we got to know more of his backstory.<br />• THERE IS A DOG. (It does not die.) PUPPYYYYYY.<br />• I love Crow. &lt;3 I'm glad he stopped being a lying strudel and actually got fiercely protective of Han. You and me both, Crow.<br />• Raisa's battle tendencies are adorable.<br />• Raisa for world ruler!<br />• I love this fantasy world. LOVE IT.<br />• Also I love the diversity of ethnicity! It's so refreshing and excellent!<br /><br />...but while we're here I <b>do have a small list fo things I'm displeased about.</b> It ain't all rainbows and sunshine today, folks. But I'M STILL GIVING IT 5-STARS BECAUSE I DON'T CARE. I loved it. It made me <i>feeeeeel</i> and these are some of my favourite characters in the universe. #OTP<br /><br /><b>Small List of Dislikes:</b><br />• Not enough people...died. (Sorry...)<br />• I just needed to be more SCARED for their lives and I really wasn't.<br />• It did drag in the middle. 600 pages is just too long yes?<br />• Amon really didn't play a big part and I think that's sad because he's spent the last 3 books being a HUGE part of Raisa's life and now he's just??? Not really???<br />• Skimmed over torture scenes = hmph.<br />• It wasn't NEARLY as funny as the first 3 books. Where are all my jokes and quips??<br /><br /><br /><b>ALL IN ALL:</b> This has got to be one of my favourite fantasy series OF ALL TIME. I wish it was better known!! I NEED SOMEONE TO FLAIL WITH OMG. I am an infinite fan of the magic system, Han/Raisa and basically I aggressively ship them like NO OTHER, and I love the world and the outcome and the detail of the history. The Demon King and the Wolf Queen = the <i>best thing of ever</i>.<br /><br />Honestly I can't recommend this enough.<br /><br />I LOVE IT AS MUCH AS I LOVE CAKE.<br /><br />Okay <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23253083.Flamecaster__Shattered_Realms___1_" title="Flamecaster (Shattered Realms, #1) by Cinda Williams Chima" rel="nofollow noopener">Flamecaster</a>...COME TO ME NOW PRECIOUS.<br /><br /><br /><br /><blockquote>"What are you planning to do?" Raisa said.<br />"Marry you, if you'll have me." He looked into her eyes. "I promise you that if you agree to marry me, I will make it happen."<br />"That won't make anybody happy," Raisa said.<br />"Except for the two of us," Han said. He grinned. "And maybe Dog."</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="6117037673463103603" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8553435298663414564">Ahhh you guys... this was <b>amazing. </b> Ok but first I must fangirl..<br/><br/><b>That. Dance. Scene. </b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467907189ra/19645059.gif' width='300px' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Holy blazers. <br/><br/>This isn't going to be a long review... but I hope to express just how <b>epic</b> this journey has been.I'm not even kidding... I got teary eyed at the end. <br/><br/>-Mild Spoilers-<br/><br/>Raisa's journey has been incredible. She is a heroine that I seriously LOVED rooting for. I was not at all disappointed as her journey came to a close. I felt so connected to her and in the end I just wanted all her sacrifices and pain</span>
  <span id="freeText8553435298663414564" style="display:none">Ahhh you guys... this was <b>amazing. </b> Ok but first I must fangirl..<br><br><b>That. Dance. Scene. </b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467907189ra/19645059.gif" width="300px" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Holy blazers. <br><br>This isn't going to be a long review... but I hope to express just how <b>epic</b> this journey has been.I'm not even kidding... I got teary eyed at the end. <br><br>-Mild Spoilers-<br><br>Raisa's journey has been incredible. She is a heroine that I seriously LOVED rooting for. I was not at all disappointed as her journey came to a close. I felt so connected to her and in the end I just wanted all her sacrifices and pain to be worth it- and it WAS.<br><br>Oh and Han. What a man. Can we just applaud him for the fact that he made Raisa wait until he married her? He refused to be a backstreet lover. He refused to watch her be married off to another man and meet her in private. He made her a vow and he kept it. And he FOUGHT for her... non stop... UGH I can't. <br><br>My only complaints are that I wanted much more of Micah (I still believe he's a good guy and he got pushed off... I mean he DID save Raisa several times...) and Amon... after all that emotional turmoil, I just feel heartbroken over him. I feel very dissatisfied with his ending... we deserved more. Also, the writing was so deep and intricate but I feel like many scenes could have been much shorter. I don't need every footstep of every journey described. But whatever... I loved this anyway. <br><br>So in the end.. this was an INCREDIBLE and emotional journey and I can't believe I waited so long to read these. <br><br><a href="http://www.herbookishthings.com" rel="nofollow noopener">My Blog</a> ~ <a href="https://www.instagram.com/reverieandink/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> ~ <a href="https://twitter.com/reverieandink" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> ~ <a href="https://www.etsy.com/shop/reverieandink" rel="nofollow noopener">Etsy</a></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer316358253" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer4391092590429002150"><b>Re-read 2016</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1459525966ra/18622540.gif' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Ha! I <i>love</i> it when a series I read years ago actually HOLDS UP!<br/>Mostly, because that means I was <i>right</i> the first time, but also because it means...<b>I WAS RIGHT</b>.<br/>Yeah. I'm that shallow.<br/>Point is, book 4 was a fantastic conclusion to the Seven Realms series, and you should definitely give these books a try. Especially if you've been on the fence about this one.<br/><b>GET OFF THE FENCE!</b><br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1459525966ra/18622541.gif' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><b>Original review: 2012</b><br/>Reading the last book in a series you love is always hard. I was so afraid this was going t</span>
  <span id="freeText4391092590429002150" style="display:none"><b>Re-read 2016</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1459525966ra/18622540.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ha! I <i>love</i> it when a series I read years ago actually HOLDS UP!<br>Mostly, because that means I was <i>right</i> the first time, but also because it means...<b>I WAS RIGHT</b>.<br>Yeah. I'm that shallow.<br>Point is, book 4 was a fantastic conclusion to the Seven Realms series, and you should definitely give these books a try. Especially if you've been on the fence about this one.<br><b>GET OFF THE FENCE!</b><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1459525966ra/18622541.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>Original review: 2012</b><br>Reading the last book in a series you love is always hard. I was so afraid this was going to be a disappointment (<i><b>Mockingjay</b>, I'm talking to you</i>), but I couldn't be happier with the way Chima wrapped things up.<br>5 big fat stars!<br>The only thing I can't understand is why <i>none</i> of my GR friends have read any of these books.<br>???<br><i>
  <b>What is wrong with you people?!</b>
</i><br><br>The Crimson Crown is a wonderful ending to the Seven Realms books, but if the author wants to...<br>*<i>hint, hint</i>*<br>there's still plenty of room to write a few more books in this world.<br><i>I</i>, for one, would love to continue reading about all of the characters Chima has created.<br>Dancer, Micah, Melody, Cat, Willo..<br>Really, there are so many stories left to tell in the Seven Realms, that I refuse to believe this is the end!<br><br>If you haven't picked up these books yet, you don't know what you're missing. <br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6342491.The_Demon_King__Seven_Realms___1_" title="The Demon King (Seven Realms, #1) by Cinda Williams Chima" rel="nofollow noopener">The Demon King</a>.<br>Read it.<br>Now!</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2065562400" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer16471862578199574957"><b>Raisa is finally queen</b> *offically crowned but queen of my heart forever* and she's doing good. Really good. <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I have the life I want,” Raisa said. “Oh, I know it’s not perfect, and people are trying to kill me, and nobody in the queendom can get along, and we’ll likely be invaded soon, but other than that…”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>She really is. Except for the whole....<br/>The <b>wizards and clans</b> continue to fight and blame the other, wizards treating them like slaves and clans refusing to make more metals&give the</span>
  <span id="freeText16471862578199574957" style="display:none"><b>Raisa is finally queen</b> *offically crowned but queen of my heart forever* and she's doing good. Really good. <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I have the life I want,” Raisa said. “Oh, I know it’s not perfect, and people are trying to kill me, and nobody in the queendom can get along, and we’ll likely be invaded soon, but other than that…”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>She really is. Except for the whole....<br>The <b>wizards and clans</b> continue to fight and blame the other, wizards treating them like slaves and clans refusing to make more metals&amp;give the wizards more power<br>The <b>average folk</b> are adjusting to a new queen who is young but <u>murders</u> are on the rise. <br>The <b>wizard counsel</b> wants a queen easy to maneuver and the clans want a queen who will fight but only fight the wizards. <br><b>War in the south</b> is coming closer, all princes claiming to be king and willing to kill or enslave Raisa's people to make it true till suddenly! They're in the castle THEY ARE IN THE MOTHERFUCKING CASTLE PEOPLE!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1605654926ra/30391554.gif" width="170" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1605654926ra/30391554.gif" width="170" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But Raisa takes all of this with her usual sass and ass-kicking abilities. <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I just hope he doesn’t expect me to marry Kip,” Raisa said, shuddering. “I’d leap from the tower first.”<br>Cat snickered, and that set Magret to laughing, and soon they were all in convulsions.<br>“Even w-worse,” Cat cackled, blotting tears of mirth from her eyes. “Maybe he wants you to marry b-b-both of them.”<br>“I’ll make you a rope, Your Majesty, so you can hang yourself,” Magret said.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>Han</b> found out her true identity and doesn't trust her but wants to be closer. Wizard teacher thinks Han is on her side, clans are trying to control Han, <b>the Demon King's spirit</b> is trying to possess Han AND NOW HE IS BEING BLAMED FoR MURDERS. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1605654926ra/30391553.gif" width="170" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But don't worry, he and Raisa are gonna do just fine <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Finally, he knelt beside it. “I told you to stay!” he muttered. “Don’t you ever listen?”<br>This was so ludicrous, the dog such an unexpected walk-on, that Raisa couldn’t help laughing, though her eyes were blurred with tears.<br>“A dog? You’re a wanted man, accused of treason, and you brought a dog into this?” She shook her head. “Is that fair to the dog?”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1520137145ra/25158458.gif" width="170" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> Definitely recommend this book/series! The characters are dynamic in that you are really able to relate to them and connect to them. You have to keep reading because you wanna see what they do next, not just to find out the ending. While the first book is acknowledging a slow burn, try to read to the second to really see how the book builds up its plot, provides interesting character dynamics, and just a whole lotta sass.</span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12842423-jessica?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12842423-jessica?shelf=wishlist">wishlist</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1184488930" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16285826179307534988">Man oh man. This series... The Seven Realms series definitely makes my favorites list!<br/>Read this series!<br/><br/><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[<br/>I loved everything about this book.<br/>I loved that Lucious could finally find some peace... although it was pretty disappointing to hear that he was the one that betrayed Alger.. I always liked Lucious and it was just sad to hear about that. At the same time though we learned that Hanalea DIDN'T betray him, so there's that. The ending with Han brining her as a wolf to meet with Alge</span></span>
  <span id="freeText16285826179307534988" style="display:none">Man oh man. This series... The Seven Realms series definitely makes my favorites list!<br />Read this series!<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />I loved everything about this book.<br />I loved that Lucious could finally find some peace... although it was pretty disappointing to hear that he was the one that betrayed Alger.. I always liked Lucious and it was just sad to hear about that. At the same time though we learned that Hanalea DIDN'T betray him, so there's that. The ending with Han brining her as a wolf to meet with Alger was just perfect.<br /><br />I loved all of the parts with Crow and Han in this book, where as I kind of lost my patience with Crow in the past books. Especially before I knew who Crow really was. Han definitely couldn't have survived without him in this book. With the information about the underground tunnels, the treasure, everything. The part when Crow was trying to switch in and out with Han while he was being tortured had me in tears. He had already been tortured to death once, yet he tried to help Han as much as he could.<br /><br />I definitely didn't see the whole ending with Nightwalker happening. I knew that he hated Wizards so it's not crazy to think he had been killing them all... I guess I just never realized how badly he just wanted to marry Raisa more for the position than for her. I actually did think he had real feelings for her.. maybe because of their past. I was SO angry at the end after EVERYTHING that was happening.. he seriously had the nerve to try and kill Raisa. I was so happy when Night Bird took him out. Of course, I also teared up when she died. She was so young, but I'm happy that she could die in honor. <br /><br />I'm not really surprised that only Micah survived out of the Bayar family. I do feel a LITTLE bit of pity for him.. even though I still don't really like him. What did you all think about the news of Dancer being a Bayar? I'm happy that Willo came forth and showed the council what kind of trash Gavan really was. <br /><br />Of course, I'm thrilled that Han and Raisa are finally together. I was getting so angry with Raisa's father and grandmother when they were acting like they would kill him if Raisa thought about marrying him.. then Dancer explained what he knew about the amulet they gave Han. Dancer is a hero. The way he can connect with nature and the way he can work with amulets and make his own flash craft is amazing! I love him &lt;3<br /><br />Such an amazing series! Will definitely read more by Cinda Williams Chima in the future!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

<div id="review_278954805" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Rebecca" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7787321-rebecca"><img alt="Rebecca" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1358801648p2/7787321.jpg" /></a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

<div id="review_999307599" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/999307599" />
    <a title="Dorreh" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22599584-dorreh"><img alt="Dorreh" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1565727363p2/22599584.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/999307599?book_show_action=true">Jul 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dorreh" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dorreh" href="/user/show/22599584-dorreh">Dorreh</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer999307599" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17304904545057934855">You know those times in life when you feel this deep chasm in your soul and all the emotions get sucked into it? That's what this book did for me. <br/>This whole series was beautiful. From the first book it was a crescendo of ideas that were so exhilarating at some points of the book my excitement came out of me in waves. So you can only imagine what happened to me when this series ended so amazingly. <br/>There are truly no word to describe how much love I felt for the characters, and the exhilarating c</span>
  <span id="freeText17304904545057934855" style="display:none">You know those times in life when you feel this deep chasm in your soul and all the emotions get sucked into it? That's what this book did for me. <br />This whole series was beautiful. From the first book it was a crescendo of ideas that were so exhilarating at some points of the book my excitement came out of me in waves. So you can only imagine what happened to me when this series ended so amazingly. <br />There are truly no word to describe how much love I felt for the characters, and the exhilarating consequences of their lives. Normally politics in books and stories bores me, but not in this case, everything about the way the events were played out made them interesting. <br />I'm normally never satisfied with the way series end. There's always that pang of regret after mulling over a story for so long, but after a really long while, this series surprised me. After being so good, I was waiting for the moment I would be disappointed, and then it didn't happen and I was like......."omgggggggg". Yup pretty much how I feel, a holy mess of emotions.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17304904545057934855" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1579346233" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1579346233" />
    <a title="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8422853-chelsea-peril-please"><img alt="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1570038444p2/8422853.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1579346233?book_show_action=true">Mar 14, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " href="/user/show/8422853-chelsea-peril-please">Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=physical-book-wishlist-want-it-need">physical-book-wishlist-want-it-need</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=my-favorite-covers">my-favorite-covers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=awesome-heroines">awesome-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=absolute-favorites">absolute-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=could-read-over-and-over-again">could-read-over-and-over-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=alternating-pov">alternating-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=unforgettable-male-leads">unforgettable-male-leads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=epic-reads-for-light-and-dark-pup">epic-reads-for-light-and-dark-pup</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1579346233" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4238551641379599158"><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote> "He's the one steps away, right?" she said. "He knows this is dangerous turf-for both of you. He won't make his move until he knows he can win it all."<br/>"But what if that never happens?" Raisa said.<br/>"He won't settle," Cat said. "He'll wait forever if need be."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1301.photobucket.com/user/ChelseaRoberts3/media/tumblr_o1cnfjyEyF1ts69tto1_r1_500_zps272lansg.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1459348088ra/18600506.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_o1cnfjyEyF1ts69tto1_r1_500_zps272lansg.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Man..I was so excited about writing this review. I was so excited to show how much I loved, adored, cherished this series. But now, sitting here, finally able to type out my feelings I think….How could I possibly put into word</span>
  <span id="freeText4238551641379599158" style="display:none"><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote> "He's the one steps away, right?" she said. "He knows this is dangerous turf-for both of you. He won't make his move until he knows he can win it all."<br>"But what if that never happens?" Raisa said.<br>"He won't settle," Cat said. "He'll wait forever if need be."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1301.photobucket.com/user/ChelseaRoberts3/media/tumblr_o1cnfjyEyF1ts69tto1_r1_500_zps272lansg.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1459348088ra/18600506.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_o1cnfjyEyF1ts69tto1_r1_500_zps272lansg.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Man..I was so excited about writing this review. I was so excited to show how much I loved, adored, cherished this series. But now, sitting here, finally able to type out my feelings I think….How could I possibly put into words just how much this series meant to me? We read a book or a series and we obsess about it ceaselessly, yet when it comes time to actually put it into words? It’s virtually impossible to capture that essence of what makes us so happy, excited, unflinchingly devoted to these characters. And yet...I can’t very well not try, right?<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>That's what you do when you love someone-you notice and notice and notice.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>I mean, what’s the point, really, when so many other wonderful reviewers have done it a million times better than me and a thousand times before. What makes mine so special? Me? My review-why stop here and read this? For instance: Anna? <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1010899628?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Her review</a> is just so perfect, and it shows just how much she adores this series, but makes it <b>fun and exciting</b> with her cute little visuals and adorable accent that is translated through the thoughts on her review. It’s simple, yet portrays every gamut of emotion she felt throughout the series with out being a screeching fangirl (which she is, if I do say so myself) and spoiling everything. <b>I don’t know anyone who is more obsessed with these characters</b> (I’d like to think my obsession is only a peg below hers, but I can’t be sure-she has got it <u>bad</u>) or who took better care in representing them and presenting them in a way that people become curious, despite their level of enjoyment for fantasy. If you’re reading this review, you’re likely one of my best friends who always reads them (I know who you are and I ADORE YOU). Or, you might be someone who thinks my ramblings are worth reading every once in a while. And hey, if that’s you? I admire your tenacity, I can be a bit much to take.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>...He paused for a heartbeat, then added, "Though avoiding Nightwalker seems like a good idea to me."<br>"It's a match my father favors," Raisa said.<br>"Then your father is wrong," Han said. "Nightwalker thinks the world sprouted from his bunghole."<br>Raisa dismissed this image with some difficulty.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>But that’s my point-This series isn’t simply about the adventures or the romance or the peril and action that shape how the throne is ruled and the towns destroyed-<u>It’s so much more than that</u>. It’s the soft looks between life long friends as things become complicated. <b>It’s the touch of a street thug who might just be what you’ve been looking for your entire life without even knowing it</b>. It’s the desperation shared with the person you thought you’d grow old with as that dream crumbles to ashes beneath your feet. <b>It’s a character driven series</b>. And if you don’t like, love, adore, obsess, care, or cherish these people that have been through literally every devastating thing possible…you have nothing. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote> "Haven't you heard about me?" he [Han] said, with a tight smile. "I'm really a very dangerous person." And he did look dangerous until he said, "Look, could you watch Dog for me while I'm gone?"</blockquote>
</b><br><br>And if only I can show my love of the characters, and everyone can see how much I adore them, then I guess I’ll call my review a success. I’ll admit that-I don’t always just love books that aren’t all packed to the brim with romance and peril and desperate attempts at love while things begin to disintegrate before two young lovers’ eyes. <b>I am becoming a person who adores character driven stories</b> where we get to know a person inside and out in just day-to-day life….but I’m not always on board, <i>especially</i> with fantasy. So believe me when I say this is a breath of fresh air. Literally. I mean it.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>Would she be required to sacrifice everything-every single person she cared about for this bloody throne?<br>Apparently so.</blockquote>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1301.photobucket.com/user/ChelseaRoberts3/media/tumblr_m3f7fcltHy1r3a6jho1_500_zpsu2vqk7wx.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1459347734ra/18600456.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m3f7fcltHy1r3a6jho1_500_zpsu2vqk7wx.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So much love, loss, betrayal, and heartache are bestowed upon on our young characters, and seeing them go through each and every devastating event makes the vice-like grip on your heart tighter and tighter, squeezing until you can’t hardly breathe anymore, causing you to fall deeper and harder in love with characters you were already falling head over heels for after only a few chapters in book one. <b>Raisa</b>, the proud Princess who can’t wait to help her kingdom grow and become a better place, yet doesn’t want to be forced to marry. <b>Amon</b>, her best friend and soldier, the guy who would do anything to protect Raisa and the throne-even forfeit his own life. And so many more just like this…but none quite like <b>Han.</b><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>He reached over and closed his hands over hers, the first time he'd dare touch her. He looked into her eyes. "This may sound arrogant, and I'm sorry if it does, but you're so alone, Raisa, and so am I. Didn't you ever wish you could have a...a partner? A friend? Somebody you could say anything to-where you didn't have to pick and choose words like a merchant at a market? Someone who wants you for yourself?"</blockquote>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1301.photobucket.com/user/ChelseaRoberts3/media/tumblr_m8idvw1yS51qd9agqo4_500_zpsy9d07j05.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1459347734ra/18600457.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m8idvw1yS51qd9agqo4_500_zpsy9d07j05.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Han, who is many things without being conceited. Han, who would do ANYTHING to protect those he loved…even as that count becomes smaller and smaller, Raisa being his number one priority. Han, <b>who makes your stomach drop and your heart beat way too fast</b> with a simple smile, haunted eyes, a quick joke, his loyalty, his misguided love for Raisa becoming the real and true thing…Even if it wasn’t what he ever wanted or planned for. But that’s the thing about Han, you know?? <b>He never wanted these things</b> coming his way, yet he excels, he thrives, he becomes the best he can be-For he won’t settle for less…He wants <u>
  <b>everything</b>
</u>. And that includes the girl who stole his heart right from underneath his feet. He’s used to being the thief…but as it turns out, she invaded his heart from the beginning, <b>stealing his heart</b> before he knew what happened to him.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>He closed his eyes, breathed in, opened his eyes again as if to assure himself she was still there. "I want to breathe you in for the rest of my life."</blockquote>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1301.photobucket.com/user/ChelseaRoberts3/media/tumblr_mqqvwr5XpY1rj4uo2o1_500_zpshsrgfhbu.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1459347734ra/18600458.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mqqvwr5XpY1rj4uo2o1_500_zpshsrgfhbu.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So, as you see, this isn’t the best review, but I loved these characters. They mean so much to me-every one of them. I can’t wait to someday get these gorgeous hardbacks for my shelf, and I can’t wait to re-read them again with my Han loving (creepily obsessed?) buddy who loves our random (and frequent) gush sessions about all things Seven Realms (okay, mostly Han, shut up). But, for now, I have to live with being tired 24/7 and having to finish this series much quicker than I wanted to and in less than desirable circumstances. It sucks, but that’s what re-reads are for. <b>I didn’t get to enjoy the last three books as much as I’d have wanted to</b>, real life and all that jazz, but it didn’t stunt my enjoyment, and that’s really saying something. So, for those of you still reading (doubtful), I hope that my love for these characters is enough to excite you and nudge you into giving Han’s journey a try. If not, oh well, more Han for me. <br><br><br><b>*Re-written seeing as my laptop shut off randomly for no reason whatsoever, just…UGH I’m too tired to care about making it all perfect again, so it isn’t nearly as good. So sad.*</b><br><br><br><i>For more of my reviews, please visit:</i><br><a href="http://starcrossedbookblog.com/chelsea-peril-please-reviews/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452287303i/17673713._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a title="Facebook" href="https://www.facebook.com/starcrossedbookblog" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438055977i/15660595.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a title="Twitter" href="https://twitter.com/starcrossedblog" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438055639i/15660580.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a title="RSS" href="http://feeds.feedburner.com/starcrossedbookblog/METU" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438055639i/15660581.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a title="BLOGLOVIN" href="https://www.bloglovin.com/blogs/star-crossed-book-blog-13035961" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438055639i/15660579.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a title="Google+" href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/b/116866754719786372049/+Starcrossedbookblog/posts" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439651670i/15866819.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>**************************<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Would she be required to sacrifice everything-every single person she cared about for this bloody throne?<br>Apparently so.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Oh. My. Gahd. This series was beautiful, fantastic, other-worldy in <b>it's ability to pull you in and wish you never had to let go</b>. These characters (HAN!) have embedded themselves into my heart forever, and I will not likely forget them soon. Raisa and Han and Amon and Dancer and Cat...I can't even. And Han's loyalty (and Raisa's, for that matter) made my heart stutter with undiluted joy and cheer even when all hope was lost. <br><br>What started out as a curiosity on my part has became something that I:<br><br>A) MUST have on my bookshelf (Aaahhh Christmas will be a salty one indeed)<br>B) Will have to re-read again, and SOON<br>C) Will never forget <br>D) Will forever consider a favorite<br><br>Thanks to Jen for the gentle nudge by buying the first book for me for Christmas this year, and a begrudging thanks to the Snake that all but pushed me off the cliff. You both ROCK ♥<br><br><br>RTC when I can! Because....HAN! :P<br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="4238551641379599158" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1905494771" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1905494771" />
    <a title="Caitlin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/57334157-caitlin"><img alt="Caitlin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1507948675p2/57334157.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1905494771?book_show_action=true">Mar 26, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Caitlin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Caitlin" href="/user/show/57334157-caitlin">Caitlin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57334157-caitlin?shelf=2017-read">2017-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57334157-caitlin?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57334157-caitlin?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1905494771" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3159794053303179804"><i>
  <b>"So many questions, so many stories that needed telling. A story of their own they needed to write. One with a happy ending."</b>
</i><br/><br/>I finished this book about a week ago and I still don't know how to write coherent sentences about how much I loved this book and this series. When I finished I was honestly in tears of happiness. It was a perfect conclusion to an absolutely amazing series. I'm just so happy and content with where this series went. I honestly cannot recommend it enough. <br/><br/>Let's just talk</span>
  <span id="freeText3159794053303179804" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>"So many questions, so many stories that needed telling. A story of their own they needed to write. One with a happy ending."</b>
</i><br /><br />I finished this book about a week ago and I still don't know how to write coherent sentences about how much I loved this book and this series. When I finished I was honestly in tears of happiness. It was a perfect conclusion to an absolutely amazing series. I'm just so happy and content with where this series went. I honestly cannot recommend it enough. <br /><br />Let's just talk about the dance scene at the beginning of this book because DAMN I WAS DEAD. Raisa and Han are just the best representation of the demon king and the original grey wolf queen, Hanalea. Also I loved Han constantly playing the role of the demon king because he really is so much like him - not in a bad way don't worry. Basically all of these rumours came up around the demon king centuries ago and they're all pretty much bullshit and that's such a good representation of Han. He's underestimated and made into someone he's not.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Oh, I am getting married," Raisa said sleepily. "You promised me that if I agreed to marry you, that you would make it happen." She extended her hand, the one with the ring Han had given her, and waved it under his nose. "So. It's time to pay up.” </i>
</b><br /><br />I absolutely adored our 2 main characters in this book but I did still want a bit more from some of the side characters. I've said it before, but Han was a character that I didn't overly care about in <i>The Demon King</i> but I definitely grew to absolutely love him throughout this series. He's just a precious little cinnamon roll and I love him endlessly. Raisa was instantly my favourite character when I first picked up this series and my love for her has just grown. She reminds me of Cleo from the <i>Falling Kingdoms</i> series and I could instantly see her potential - she wasn't just a spoilt princess that everyone made her out to be. She has some serious guts and she makes an incredible Queen. Together this ship is just amazing. I love them together - although I wish there was more of them together. <br /><br />I would have liked to see more of Amon being happy. I mean I guess we don't really know if he is happy with his arranged marriage wife - I hope they are because he deserves the world. Honestly, I'm still shocked that he didn't die. I was pretty certain that he was going to die sometimes throughout this series but I'm pretty happy that he lived. Dancer gave me an absolute heart attack so many times in this book but thank fucking god he's all good because I can't cope with character deaths. I wanted to absolutely kill Gavan Bayar from page 1 (thank god he died) and I still feel incredibly sorry for Fiona. She had potential and I feel like something else could have been done for her character. Poor girl. But, I wanted more from Micah. He has so much potential as a character and I feel like he didn't do as much as I wanted him to. Hopefully in the spin off we see more of him because I need him to be helpful and not a piece of shit. I HAVE HOPE FOR YOU MICAH. YOU'RE JUST UNDERESTIMATED BUT I UNDERSTAND YOU. I'm so happy that Crow got his happy ending too and the way this book ended was so sweet and I'm feeling all the feels.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Crow walked toward her, arms outstretched like a man in a dream, which he was, in a way. Sometimes a dream is enough.”</i>
</b><br /><br />As always, a shit tonne of stuff happens in this book and I was honestly stressed for the entirely of this book. I just love this series ok. </span>
  <a data-text-id="3159794053303179804" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_656204943" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/656204943" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/656204943?book_show_action=true">Jul 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Anyone wanting to try out fantasy, or those who have only read bad fantasy</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Stacia (the 2010 club) by: </span>
      Buddy read with Sandra and Robin
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=action-and-adventure">action-and-adventure</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=multiple-pov">multiple-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=favorite-book-guys">favorite-book-guys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=casters-or-witches">casters-or-witches</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=male-pov">male-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=epic-or-high-fantasy">epic-or-high-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer656204943" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17222302255845219052"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Everything's a risk."</i>
    <b></b>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>In the Seven Realms, truer words have never been spoken.<br/><br/><b>4.5 stars</b> I'm so sad to see the <i>Seven Realms</i> series come to an end.<br/><br/><b>Mystery! Intrigue! Adventure! Danger! Magic! Fighting! Forbidden Love!</b> How many rounds of awesome can we squeeze into one book? I don't know the final tally but the count is high (along with the dead bodies). <br/><br/>Han is incredible. Were it not for him, this series wouldn't have had the same edge to it. Everyone likes to root for the underdo</span>
  <span id="freeText17222302255845219052" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Everything's a risk."</i>
    <b></b>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />In the Seven Realms, truer words have never been spoken.<br /><br /><b>4.5 stars</b> I'm so sad to see the <i>Seven Realms</i> series come to an end.<br /><br /><b>Mystery! Intrigue! Adventure! Danger! Magic! Fighting! Forbidden Love!</b> How many rounds of awesome can we squeeze into one book? I don't know the final tally but the count is high (along with the dead bodies). <br /><br />Han is incredible. Were it not for him, this series wouldn't have had the same edge to it. Everyone likes to root for the underdog, and Han had a full deck stacked against him. His ability to take repeated life-beatings and keep on pushing forward endeared him to many a reader. <br /><br />And it didn't hurt that he had crazy ninja skills.<br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>As if in answer to her prayers, someone swarmed across the ceiling of the cathedral, swinging from one fixture to another, finding handholds where none existed. He dangled over their heads, arrows pinging all around him, then dropped to the floor.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br />I'm still a softie for Amon though. I like those protective types. Always have. Maybe he wasn't all magic flash and ninja technique, but he'll always have a place in my heart. I wish <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[he'd almost had his own part of the story, since he was such a focus in the first book. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />The best part about <i>Crimson Crown</i> was that it gave us plenty of happy without crossing every t and dotting every i. We got enough to satisfy without knowing exactly how everything in the future would be laid out. <br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I want to breathe you in for the rest of my life."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />Few authors know how to end a series right and this is one of them. Happy cheer for a job well done!<br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Sometimes a dream is enough.</i>
    <b></b>
  </b>
</blockquote></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1543317710" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16891207503255047550">MY BLOG: <a href='http://melissa413readsalot.blogspot.com/2016/02/the-crimson-crown-by-cinda-williams.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Melissa Martin's Reading List</a><br/><br/>Wow! It's the end..... I know this series has been out for some time, but still. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1455066937i/18050336._SX540_.jpg' alt=' : ' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>So Raisa is Queen and people are trying to tell her what to do, kill her, marry her off....blah blah blah. She's having none of that! <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455066937ra/18050337.gif' alt=' ' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Raisa and Han are still trying to find their place with each other. Hmmm... I can't give out spoiler so I can't mention that.. crap. Let's just say they want to be together still but it's a hot mess. <br/><br/>Raisa is trying to incorporate the wizards and </span>
  <span id="freeText16891207503255047550" style="display:none">MY BLOG: <a href="http://melissa413readsalot.blogspot.com/2016/02/the-crimson-crown-by-cinda-williams.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Melissa Martin's Reading List</a><br><br>Wow! It's the end..... I know this series has been out for some time, but still. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1455066937i/18050336._SX540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So Raisa is Queen and people are trying to tell her what to do, kill her, marry her off....blah blah blah. She's having none of that! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455066937ra/18050337.gif" alt=" " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Raisa and Han are still trying to find their place with each other. Hmmm... I can't give out spoiler so I can't mention that.. crap. Let's just say they want to be together still but it's a hot mess. <br><br>Raisa is trying to incorporate the wizards and the magic users into the kingdom. She wants to have a kingdom where everyone gets along. Good luck with that, but she doesn't give up. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1455066937i/18050338.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>AND that stupid Lord Bayar is still causing trouble and he is just evil, so damn evil. He should have been called the demon king! He does some really bad stuff in this book, but he gets his time and he gets it in a rather lovely way :-) <br><br>Oh oh, there is this really cool part where Bayer gets put in his place. Its' a MILD SPOILER SO... <br><br><b>
  <i>"Excuse me?" Lord Bayar said, "What did you say?"<br>"I vote for Hanson Alister for High Wizard, to replace you," Gryphon said. "I believe that means he wins."</i>
</b><br><br>I love it, some other really cool stuff happens in that meeting but I will leave it to you to read. It's one of those happy dance, in your face jerk, kind of moments. :-) <br><br>I liked Gryphon's character, we find out some stuff about him in the book, it's sad and eye opening as well. Poor guy. And I love Dancer even more in this book when I find out more about him. And there is Cat.. the list goes on, there are a few great people in the book. <br><br>Anyhoo, not only are people trying to kill the Queen, they are trying to frame Han for all kinds of wizard deaths and putting things around that make him look like the one. And you know.. I never would have thunk who it turned out to be. 0_0<br><br>We also get to find out the secrets of the Demon King. There is a whole bunch of stuff that opens up with that revelation. It was a "wait what?" moment for me. <br><br>All I have left to say is that the four books in this series are awesome and if you have been thinking of reading them, just do it. <br><br><b>
  <i>The Gray Wolf Queens live on as wolves.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455066937ra/18050339.gif" alt=" " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Freaking makes me tear up me being a wolf lover... the queens will always be there.......<br><br>Last sentence in the book ↓<br><br><b>Sometimes a dream is enough.</b><br><br>I believe that with all my heart and soul! </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

<span id="freeTextContainer965491123453993967">This has been such an amazing, compelling ride. I started the series earlier this year and I’m so so glad to have made that decision. Following Han and Raisa was long and occasionally difficult but the end results are completely worth it. This world is so well thought out and it makes me happy to know there’s a companion series that I can start now that I’ve finished the Seven Realms! </span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13682027-ann-annreads?shelf=own">own</a>,

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1939158544" class="readable"
